//REGION Add Skill and Level Checks
QRY
Xorn_CharacterIsPlayer((CHARACTERGUID)_Char)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Char)
THEN
DB_NOOP(1);

IF
CharacterUnlockedTalent((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover")
THEN
QuestAdd(_Char, "Xorn_Runic_Arsenal_Crafting");
ObjectSetFlag(_Char, "QuestUpdate_Xorn_Runic_Arsenal_Crafting_Xorn_Runic_Arsenal_Start");
SetTag(_Char, "Runic Arsenal");

//Tier 1

IF
GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)
AND
CharacterGetLevel(_Player, _Level)
AND
_Level < 10
AND
CharacterHasSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave", 0)
THEN
CharacterAddSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave");
ObjectSetFlag(_Player, "Runic_Weaponry");

GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)

_Level < 10

THEN

IF
GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
AND
CharacterHasSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave", 1)
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave");
ObjectClearFlag(_Player, "Runic_Weaponry");
ClearTag(_Player, "Runic Arsenal");

IF
GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
AND
CharacterHasSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Reach", 1)
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Reach");

IF
GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
AND
CharacterHasSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Sang", 1)
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Sang");
ObjectClearFlag(_Player, "Runic_Weaponry");

IF
GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
AND
CharacterHasSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T1", 1)
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T1");
ObjectClearFlag(_Player, "Runic_Weaponry");

IF
GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
AND
CharacterHasSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T1", 1)
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T1");
ObjectClearFlag(_Player, "Runic_Weaponry");

IF
CharacterUnlockedTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover")
AND
CharacterGetLevel(_Player, _Level)
AND
_Level < 10
THEN
CharacterAddSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave");
CharacterAddSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Reach");
CharacterAddSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Sang");
CharacterAddSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T1");
CharacterAddSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T1");
ItemTemplateAddTo("Xorn_Runic_Hammer_59c39a04-468a-422e-be5e-a880acb400a1", _Player, 1, 1);
ObjectSetFlag(_Player, "Runic_Weaponry");

//REGION Locked or No Talent Removals
IF
GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_CleaveT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_CleaveT3");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Reach");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_ReachT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_ReachT3");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Sang");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_SangT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_SangT3");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T1");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T3");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T1");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Player, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T3");
ItemTemplateRemoveFrom("Xorn_Runic_Hammer_59c39a04-468a-422e-be5e-a880acb400a1", _Player, 99);
ObjectClearFlag(_Player, "Runic_Weaponry");
ClearTag(_Player, "Runic Arsenal");

IF
CharacterLockedTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover")
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_CleaveT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_CleaveT3");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Reach");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_ReachT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_ReachT3");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Sang");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_SangT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_SangT3");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T1");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T3");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T1");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T3");
ItemTemplateRemoveFrom("Xorn_Runic_Hammer_59c39a04-468a-422e-be5e-a880acb400a1", _Char, 99);
ObjectClearFlag(_Char, "Runic_Weaponry");
ClearTag(_Char, "Runic Arsenal");

IF
CharacterLeveledUp(_Char)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)
AND
CharacterGetLevel((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Level)
AND
_Level >= 10
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Reach");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Sang");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T1");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T1");
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_CleaveT2"); 
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_ReachT2");
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_SangT2");
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T2"); 
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T2");

CharacterLeveledUp((CHARACTERGUID)_Char)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)
AND
CharacterGetLevel(_Char, _Level)
AND
_Level >= 15
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_CleaveT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_ReachT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_SangT2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T2");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T2");
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_CleaveT3"); 
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_ReachT3");
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_SangT3");
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T3"); 
CharacterAddSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T3");

// Redundancy Cleanup

IF
CharacterLeveledUp((CHARACTERGUID)_Char)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)
AND
CharacterGetLevel((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Level)
AND
_Level >= 10
THEN
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Cleave");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Reach");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Sang");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Amulet_T1");
CharacterRemoveSkill(_Char, "Shout_Xorn_Create_Runes_Armor_T1");

AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)

AND
_Level >= 15

//REGION Flagging Runes


IF
RuneRemoved((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, (ITEMGUID)_Rune, _Slot)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry_Runed", 1)
THEN
ObjectClearFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry_Runed");

IF
RuneRemoved((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, (ITEMGUID)_Rune, _Slot)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry_Runed", 1)
THEN
ObjectClearFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry_Runed");




//Rune Template Inserts

RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Cleave_STR_1_cb74fed7-6ffb-438b-baa1-67bb4091fdbc", _Slot)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)
THEN
ProcObjectTimer((ITEMGUID)_Item, "Xorn_Rune_Insert_Delay", 500);

PROC
ProcObjectTimerFinished((ITEMGUID)_Item, "Xorn_Rune_Insert_Delay")
THEN
ObjectSetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry_Runed");

//REGION Hammer Time

IF
GameStarted(_Region, _)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Player)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Player, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)
AND
ItemTemplateIsInCharacterInventory(_Player, "Xorn_Runic_Hammer_59c39a04-468a-422e-be5e-a880acb400a1", 0)
THEN
ItemTemplateAddTo("Xorn_Runic_Hammer_59c39a04-468a-422e-be5e-a880acb400a1", _Player, 1, 1); 

IF
CharacterUsedSkillOnTarget((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "Target_Xorn_Runic_Hammer", _, _)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 0)
AND
Xorn_GetRuneSlotCount(_Item, _Slots)
AND
_Slots == 0
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 3
THEN
NRD_ItemCloneBegin(_Item);
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish();
PlayEffect(_Item, "RS3_FX_Skills_Divine_Barrage_Impact_01");
ItemDestroy(_Item);

IF
CharacterUsedSkillOnTarget((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "Target_Xorn_Runic_Hammer", _, _)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 1)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 3
THEN
NRD_ItemCloneBegin(_Item);
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish2();
PlayEffect(_Item, "RS3_FX_Skills_Divine_Barrage_Impact_01");
ItemDestroy(_Item);

IF
CharacterUsedSkillOnTarget((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "Target_Xorn_Runic_Hammer", _, _)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 0)
AND
Xorn_GetRuneSlotCount(_Item, _Slots)
AND
_Slots == 0
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 4
THEN
NRD_ItemCloneBegin(_Item);
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish();
PlayEffect(_Item, "RS3_FX_Skills_Divine_Barrage_Impact_01");
ItemDestroy(_Item);

IF
CharacterUsedSkillOnTarget((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "Target_Xorn_Runic_Hammer", _, _)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 1)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 4
THEN
NRD_ItemCloneBegin(_Item);
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish2();
PlayEffect(_Item, "RS3_FX_Skills_Divine_Barrage_Impact_01");
ItemDestroy(_Item);

IF
CharacterUsedSkillOnTarget((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "Target_Xorn_Runic_Hammer", _, _)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 0)
AND
Xorn_GetRuneSlotCount(_Item, _Slots)
AND
_Slots == 0
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 1
THEN
NRD_ItemCloneBegin(_Item);
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish();
PlayEffect(_Item, "RS3_FX_Skills_Divine_Barrage_Impact_01");
ItemDestroy(_Item);

IF
CharacterUsedSkillOnTarget((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "Target_Xorn_Runic_Hammer", _, _)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 1)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 1
THEN
NRD_ItemCloneBegin(_Item);
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish2();
PlayEffect(_Item, "RS3_FX_Skills_Divine_Barrage_Impact_01");
ItemDestroy(_Item);

IF
CharacterUsedSkillOnTarget((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "Target_Xorn_Runic_Hammer", _, _)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 0)
AND

AND
_Slots == 0
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND

THEN
NRD_ItemCloneBegin(_Item);
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish();
PlayEffect(_Item, "RS3_FX_Skills_Divine_Barrage_Impact_01");

IF
CharacterUsedSkillOnTarget((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "Target_Xorn_Runic_Hammer", _, _)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 9
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 1)

NRD_ItemCloneBegin(_Item);
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish2();
PlayEffect(_Item, "RS3_FX_Skills_Divine_Barrage_Impact_01");
ItemDestroy(_Item);

//Clone Procs Rune On

PROC
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish()
AND
NRD_ItemClone(_NewItem)
AND
CharacterGetHostCharacter(_Char)
THEN
NRD_ItemSetPermanentBoostInt(_NewItem, "RuneSlots", 1);
ShowNotification(_Char, "Rune Slot Added");
ItemToInventory((ITEMGUID)_NewItem, _Char, 1, 1, 0);
ObjectSetFlag(_NewItem, "Runic_Weaponry");
CharacterAddAttribute(_Char, "Dummy", 0);

//Clone Proc Rune Off

PROC
PROC_XYZ_ItemCloneFinish2()
AND
NRD_ItemClone(_NewItem)
AND
CharacterGetHostCharacter(_Char)
THEN
NRD_ItemSetPermanentBoostInt(_NewItem, "RuneSlots", 0);
ShowNotification(_Char, "Rune Slot Removed");
ItemToInventory((ITEMGUID)_NewItem, _Char, 1, 1, 0);
ObjectClearFlag(_NewItem, "Runic_Weaponry");
CharacterAddAttribute(_Char, "Dummy", 0);

//END_REGION

//PreventEquip

IF
ItemEquipped((ITEMGUID)_Item, (CHARACTERGUID)_Char)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry", 1)
THEN
ShowNotification(_Char, "Item requires Runic Arsenal");
CharacterUnequipItem(_Char, _Item);

IF
ItemEquipped((ITEMGUID)_Item, (CHARACTERGUID)_Char)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 0)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry_Runed", 1)
THEN
ShowNotification(_Char, "Item requires Runic Arsenal");
CharacterUnequipItem(_Char, _Item);


//REGION Rune Special Effects


//REGION Vigor

IF
RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Vigor_T1_1def2bc5-ba8c-46d4-97d8-6c0983f03c4f", 0)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 9
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Vigor", -1.0);

IF
RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Vigor_T1_1def2bc5-ba8c-46d4-97d8-6c0983f03c4f", 0)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value != 9
AND
ItemRemoveRune(_Char, _Item, 0, (ITEMGUID)_Rune)
THEN
ShowNotification(_Char, "Rune not Intended for this Item Type");

IF
RuneRemoved((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, (ITEMGUID)_Rune, 0)
AND
GetTemplate(_Rune, _Template)
AND
_Template == "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Vigor_T1_1def2bc5-ba8c-46d4-97d8-6c0983f03c4f"
THEN
RemoveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Vigor");

IF
RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Vigor_T1_CON_1882b637-c6a3-4676-a2bc-f4410d849141", 0)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 9
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Vigor", -1.0);

IF
RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Vigor_T1_CON_1882b637-c6a3-4676-a2bc-f4410d849141", 0)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value != 9
AND
ItemRemoveRune(_Char, _Item, 0, (ITEMGUID)_Rune)
THEN
ShowNotification(_Char, "Rune not Intended for this Item Type");

IF
RuneRemoved((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, (ITEMGUID)_Rune, 0)
AND
GetTemplate(_Rune, _Template)
AND
_Template == "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Vigor_T1_CON_1882b637-c6a3-4676-a2bc-f4410d849141"
THEN
RemoveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Vigor");

IF
RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Vigor_T1_FIN_df07c23f-de2d-4a1f-a00c-3ab6d03794ee", 0)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 9
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Vigor", -1.0);

IF
RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Vigor_T1_FIN_df07c23f-de2d-4a1f-a00c-3ab6d03794ee", 0)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value != 9
AND
ItemRemoveRune(_Char, _Item, 0, (ITEMGUID)_Rune)
THEN
ShowNotification(_Char, "Rune not Intended for this Item Type");

IF
RuneRemoved((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, (ITEMGUID)_Rune, 0)

//Vigor Status

IF
CharacterStatusApplied((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "DECAYING_TOUCH", _)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Vigor", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_NoLoop", 0)
AND
GetStatusTurns(_Char, "DECAYING_TOUCH", _Turns)
AND
IntegerSubtract(_Turns, 1, _Turns2)
AND
Real(_Turns2, _Turns_R)
AND
RealProduct(_Turns_R, 6.0, _Result)
AND
_Result >= 6.0
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "DECAYING_TOUCH", _Result);

IF
CharacterStatusApplied((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "DECAYING_TOUCH", _)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Vigor", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_NoLoop", 0)
AND
GetStatusTurns(_Char, "DECAYING_TOUCH", _Turns)
AND
IntegerSubtract(_Turns, 1, _Turns2)
AND
Real(_Turns2, _Turns_R)
AND
RealProduct(_Turns_R, 6.0, _Result)
AND
_Result <= 5.9
THEN
RemoveStatus(_Char, "DECAYING_TOUCH");
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_NoLoop", 6.0);

IF
NRD_OnStatusAttempt((CHARACTERGUID)_Target, "DECAYING_TOUCH", _Handle, (GUIDSTRING)_Instigator)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Target, "Xorn_Rune_Vigor", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Target, "Xorn_NoLoop", 1)
THEN
NRD_StatusPreventApply(_Target, _Handle, 1);

//ASMOSStatus

IF
NRD_OnPrepareHit((CHARACTERGUID)_Defender, _Attacker, _Damage, _Handle)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Defender, "Xorn_Rune_Asmos", 1)
AND
NRD_HitGetInt(_Handle, "HitType", _HitType)
AND
_HitType == 6
AND
DB_XornAsmos(_DamageType)
AND
NRD_HitGetDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _Value)
AND
IntegerDivide(_Value, 2, _NewValue)
THEN
NRD_HitClearDamage(_Handle, _DamageType);
NRD_HitAddDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _NewValue);

IF
NRD_OnPrepareHit((CHARACTERGUID)_Defender, _Attacker, _Damage, _Handle)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Defender, "Xorn_Rune_Asmos2", 1)
AND
NRD_HitGetInt(_Handle, "HitType", _HitType)
AND
_HitType == 6
AND
DB_XornAsmos(_DamageType)
AND
NRD_HitGetDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _Value)
AND
IntegerDivide(_Value, 3, _NewValue)
THEN
NRD_HitClearDamage(_Handle, _DamageType);
NRD_HitAddDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _NewValue);

IF
NRD_OnPrepareHit((CHARACTERGUID)_Defender, _Attacker, _Damage, _Handle)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Defender, "Xorn_Rune_Asmos3", 1)
AND

//TALISMANStatus

IF
NRD_OnPrepareHit((CHARACTERGUID)_Target, (CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Damage, _Handle)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Talisman", 1)
AND
NRD_HitGetInt(_Handle, "HitType", _HitType)
AND
DB_XornTalis(_HitType)
AND
CharacterGetEquippedItem(_Char, "Weapon", (ITEMGUID)_Item)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "IsTwoHanded", _Value)
AND
_Value == 0
AND
DB_XornAsmos(_DamageType)
AND
NRD_HitGetDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _DamageAmount)
AND
_DamageAmount > 0
AND
IntegerSum(_DamageAmount, 10, _NewDamageAmount)
THEN
NRD_HitClearDamage(_Handle, _DamageType);
NRD_HitAddDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _NewDamageAmount);

IF
NRD_OnPrepareHit((CHARACTERGUID)_Target, (CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Damage, _Handle)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Talisman", 1)
AND
NRD_HitGetInt(_Handle, "HitType", _HitType)

_Value == 1
AND
DB_XornAsmos(_DamageType)
AND
NRD_HitGetDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _DamageAmount)

_DamageAmount > 0
AND

THEN
NRD_HitClearDamage(_Handle, _DamageType);

//SHIELDStatus

IF
NRD_OnPrepareHit((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (CHARACTERGUID)_Attacker, _Damage, _Handle)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On", 1)
AND
DB_XornShielding(_DamageType)
AND
NRD_HitGetDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _DamageAmount)
AND
Real(_DamageAmount, _DamageAmountR)
AND
RealDivide(75.0, 100.0, _DResult)
AND
RealProduct(_DamageAmountR, _DResult, _Result)
AND
Integer(_Result, _ResultI)
THEN
NRD_HitClearDamage(_Handle, _DamageType);
NRD_HitAddDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _ResultI);
ProcObjectTimer((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "ShieldOn", 1000);

PROC
ProcObjectTimerFinished((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "ShieldOn")
THEN
RemoveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On");


IF
NRD_OnPrepareHit((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (CHARACTERGUID)_Attacker, _Damage, _Handle)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On2", 1)
AND
DB_XornShielding(_DamageType)
AND
NRD_HitGetDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _DamageAmount)
AND
Real(_DamageAmount, _DamageAmountR)
AND
RealDivide(60.0, 100.0, _DResult)
AND
RealProduct(_DamageAmountR, _DResult, _Result)
AND
Integer(_Result, _ResultI)
THEN
NRD_HitClearDamage(_Handle, _DamageType);
NRD_HitAddDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _ResultI);
ProcObjectTimer((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "ShieldOn2", 1000);

PROC
ProcObjectTimerFinished((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "ShieldOn2")
THEN
RemoveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On2");

IF
NRD_OnPrepareHit((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (CHARACTERGUID)_Attacker, _Damage, _Handle)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On3", 1)
AND
DB_XornShielding(_DamageType)
AND
NRD_HitGetDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _DamageAmount)
AND
Real(_DamageAmount, _DamageAmountR)
AND
RealDivide(40.0, 100.0, _DResult)
AND
RealProduct(_DamageAmountR, _DResult, _Result)
AND
Integer(_Result, _ResultI)
THEN
NRD_HitClearDamage(_Handle, _DamageType);
NRD_HitAddDamage(_Handle, _DamageType, _ResultI);
ProcObjectTimer((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "ShieldOn3", 1000);

PROC
ProcObjectTimerFinished((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, "ShieldOn3")
THEN
RemoveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On3");


IF
CombatStarted(_)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Char)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On", 0)
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On", -1.0);

IF
CombatStarted(_)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Char)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield2", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On2", 0)
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On2", -1.0);

IF
CombatStarted(_)
AND
DB_IsPlayer(_Char)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield3", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On3", 0)
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On3", -1.0);

IF
ObjectTurnStarted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On", 0)
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On", -1.0);

IF
ObjectTurnStarted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield2", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On2", 0)
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On2", -1.0);

IF
ObjectTurnStarted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield3", 1)
AND
HasActiveStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On3", 0)
THEN
ApplyStatus(_Char, "Xorn_Rune_Shield_On3", -1.0);

//END_REGION

RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, _Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_Prys_T1_f85bf326-0135-4a96-9735-c2808a66d61d", 0)

_Value != 1
AND
_Value != 4
AND

IF
RuneInserted((CHARACTERGUID)_Char, (ITEMGUID)_Item, "LOOT_Rune_Xorn_LF_T1_b52fcf00-f6eb-44c2-91f3-aa3a556d63ea", _Slot)
AND
CharacterHasTalent(_Char, "RangerLoreArrowRecover", 1)
AND
ObjectGetFlag(_Item, "Runic_Weaponry_Runed", 1)
AND
NRD_ItemGetInt(_Item, "ItemSlot", _Value)
AND
_Value == 1
AND
ItemRemoveRune(_Char, _Item, _Slot, (ITEMGUID)_Rune)
THEN
ShowNotification(_Char, "Item cannot withstand more than one Arsenal Rune.");
